          dispItems = totalItems;
        }
        jQuery("section.blocLatestArticles div.latestArticlesCarousel").trigger('carouselize', [{
          "totalItems":totalItems,
          "dispItems":dispItems,
          "loop": false,
          "nextBtn": '<a role="button"></a>',
          "prevBtn": '<a role="button"></a>',
          "prevBtnInsert": "insertBefore",
          "nextBtnInsert": "insertAfter",
          "callback": function(e) {
            }
        }]);

        $('section.blocLatestArticles div.blocLatestArticlesHeader li').click(function(){
          $('section.blocLatestArticles div.blocLatestArticlesInner').addClass('hLoader');
          $('section.blocLatestArticles div.latestArticlesCarousel').html('');
          $('section.blocLatestArticles div.latestArticlesCarousel').css('visibility', 'hidden');
          dispItems = 6;
          $('section.blocLatestArticles div.blocLatestArticlesHeader li').removeClass("selected");
          $('section.blocLatestArticles div.blocLatestArticlesHeader div.more').removeClass("selected");
          var selectedObj = $(this);
          var tag = selectedObj.attr('tag');
          tag = tag ? tag : 0;
          $.ajax({
            type: "GET",
            url: '?ctrl=ajax_home&type=latest_articles_in_tsb&tag='+tag,
            success: function(data) {
              totalItems = $(data).find('li').size();
              var html = '<div class="latestArticlesCarousel">'+data+'</div>';
              $('section.blocLatestArticles div.blocLatestArticlesContent').html(html);

              jQuery("section.blocLatestArticles div.latestArticlesCarousel").trigger('carouselize', [{
                "totalItems":totalItems,
                "dispItems":dispItems,
                "loop": false,
                "nextBtn": '<a role="button"></a>',
                "prevBtn": '<a role="button"></a>',
                "prevBtnInsert": "insertBefore",
                "nextBtnInsert": "insertAfter",
                "callback": function(e) {
                  }
              }]);
              if(selectedObj.parent('ul').hasClass('selectCategMore')) {
                $('section.blocLatestArticles div.blocLatestArticlesHeader div.more').addClass("selected");
              }
              selectedObj.addClass("selected");
              $('section.blocLatestArticles div.blocLatestArticlesInner').removeClass('hLoader');
              $('section.blocLatestArticles div.blocLatestArticlesContent').css('visibility', 'visible');
            }
          });
        });

          <script charset="utf-8" type="text/javascript">
              var articlesData = {};
              function renderArticle(data, el){
              var link = el.attr('rel') || '';
                var inner = '';
                for (var i=0; i<data.length; i++ ) {
                  inner +='<li class="line">';
                  inner += '<a href="'+data[i].url+'" class="tListing"><span>'+data[i].titre+'<span></a>';
                  inner += '<div class="line spaceL10">';
                  inner +=  '<a href="'+data[i].url+'" class="crLink unit imgCrop imgCrop120x90"><img src="'+data[i].image+'" alt="" /></a>';
                  inner +=  '<span class="dateListing">'+data[i].datec+'</span>';
                  inner +=  '<div>'+data[i].description+'</div>';
                  inner += '</div>';
                  inner +='</li>';
                }
                $('.latestArticlesListingDatas').html(inner);
                if(el.parent('ul').hasClass('selectCategMore')) {
                  $('section.latestArticlesListing div.latestArticlesListingHeader div.more').addClass("selected bold");
                }
                el.addClass("selected bold");
                $('#seeAllLink').attr('href','#').removeAttr('onmouseover').unbind('mouseover').bind('mouseover',function(){
                  $(this).attr('href','http://www.tomshardware.com/articles/'+link).unbind('mouseover');
                });
              }
            $('section.latestArticlesListing div.latestArticlesListingHeader li').click(function(){
              $('section.blocLatestArticles div.blocLatestArticlesInner').addClass('hLoader');
              $('section.latestArticlesListing div.latestArticlesListingHeader li').removeClass("selected bold");
              $('section.latestArticlesListing div.blocLatestArticlesHeader div.more').removeClass("selected bold");
              var selectedObj = $(this);
              var tag = selectedObj.attr('tag');
              tag = tag ? tag : 0;
                if(typeof(articlesData['tag'+tag]) != 'undefined'){
                  renderArticle(articlesData['tag'+tag],selectedObj);
                } else {
                  $.ajax({
                    type: "GET",
                    dataType: 'json',
                    url: '?ctrl=ajax_home&type=latest_articles&tag='+tag+'&json=1',
                    success: function(data) {
                      articlesData['tag'+tag] = data;
                      renderArticle(data,selectedObj);
                    }
                  });
                }
            });

          </script>
        
      </section>

<script type="text/javascript">
  if(!blocNames) {
    var blocNames = new Array();
  }
  blocNames.push('blocForum');
</script>


  
  <script type="text/javascript">
    // Get the user preference cookie
    var userPrefCookieName = "UserPreference" + '18';
    var userPref = getJSONCookie(userPrefCookieName);
    var displayVal = 0;
    for(var i=0; i<blocNames.length; i++) {
      if (userPref[blocNames[i]]) {
        displayVal = userPref[blocNames[i]].displayVal;
        $('section.'+ userPref[blocNames[i]] +' div.options select.displayNResults option').removeAttr('selected');
        $('section.'+ userPref[blocNames[i]] +' div.options select.displayNResults option[value="'+displayVal+'"]').attr('selected', "selected");
      }
    }    
    
    // Display the select when the user clicks on options
    $('div.options a.optionsLink').click(function() {
      $(this).parent().find('select.displayNResults').removeClass('h');
      $(this).addClass('h');
    });
    
    // Get the json cookie
    function getJSONCookie(cookieName) {
      var start = document.cookie.indexOf(cookieName + "=");
      if (start >= 0) {
        start += cookieName.length + 1;
        var end = document.cookie.indexOf(";", start);
        if (end < 0) end = document.cookie.length;
        return JSON.parse(unescape(document.cookie.substring(start, end )));
      }
      return {};
    }
    
  </script>

            <script type="text/javascript">
              var systemBuilderUrl = "http://facebook.computing.net/cgi-bin/recent_json.pl?";
              var nbEltPerPage = 5;
              var nbOfPages = $('section.blocSystemBuilder .translateContentCommand li .translatecontent-nbPage').size();

              $.getScript(systemBuilderUrl + "?&start=0&end=" + nbEltPerPage + "&callback=" + "displaySystemBuilder");

              $('section.blocSystemBuilder .translateContentCommand li span').click(function() {
                var regExp = 'pagerGoDown|pagerGoUp|translatecontent-nbPage';
                var pagerClass = $(this).attr('class').match(regExp);
                var currentPage = $('section.blocSystemBuilder .translateContentCommand li .selected').index('section.blocSystemBuilder .translateContentCommand .translatecontent-nbPage');
                var selectedPage = 0;
                if (pagerClass!=null) {
                  switch(pagerClass[0]) {
                    case 'pagerGoDown':
                      selectedPage = (currentPage > 0) ? currentPage-1 : 0;
                      break;
                    case 'pagerGoUp':
                      selectedPage = (currentPage < nbOfPages - 1) ? currentPage+1 : nbOfPages-1;
                      break;
                    case 'translatecontent-nbPage':
                      selectedPage = $(this).index('section.blocSystemBuilder .translateContentCommand .translatecontent-nbPage');
                      break;
                    default:
                      break;
                  }
                  // Hide the content before the ajax request
                  $('section.blocSystemBuilder ul.blocSystemBuilderContent').css({'visibility': 'hidden'});
                  setTimeout('$("section.blocSystemBuilder ul.blocSystemBuilderContent").css({"visibility": "visible"});', 600);

                  var startIndex = parseInt(selectedPage*nbEltPerPage + 1);
                  var endIndex = parseInt((selectedPage*nbEltPerPage) + nbEltPerPage);
                  $.getScript(systemBuilderUrl + "?&start=" + startIndex + "&end=" + endIndex + "&callback=" + "displaySystemBuilder");

                  if (selectedPage==nbOfPages-1) {
                    $('section.blocSystemBuilder .translateContentCommand li .pagerGoUp').addClass("disabled");
                  }
                  else {
                    $('section.blocSystemBuilder .translateContentCommand li .pagerGoUp').removeClass("disabled");
                  }
                  if (selectedPage==0) {
                    $('section.blocSystemBuilder .translateContentCommand li .pagerGoDown').addClass("disabled");
                  }
                  else {
                    $('section.blocSystemBuilder .translateContentCommand li .pagerGoDown').removeClass("disabled");
                  }
                  $('section.blocSystemBuilder .translateContentCommand li span').removeClass("selected");
                  $('section.blocSystemBuilder .translateContentCommand .translatecontent-nbPage').eq(selectedPage).addClass("selected");
                }
              });

              function displaySystemBuilder(data) {
                var microTemplateParams = {};
                microTemplateParams.content = data.builds;
                $('section.blocSystemBuilder ul.blocSystemBuilderContent').html(BOM.Utils.templating.render('systemBuilderTpl', microTemplateParams));
              }
            </script>
          
        </section>

  <script type="text/javascript">
    if(!userPrefCookieName) {
      var userPrefCookieName = "UserPreference" + '18';
    }
    // Trigger the ajax request when clicked on an option in order to display the wanted number of results
    $('div.options select.displayNResults').change(function() {
      var regExp = 'blocNews|blocForum';
      var displayVal = parseInt($(this).find("option:selected").val());
      var sectionId = $(this).parents('section').eq(0).attr('class').match(regExp);
      var userPref = getJSONCookie(userPrefCookieName);
      var currentPage = 0;

      if ( sectionId!=null ) {
        var microTemplateId = '';
        var ajaxUrl = '';
        var pagerVar = null;
        var blocToReplace = '';
        var dataType = '';
        switch(sectionId[0]) {
          case 'blocNews':
            pagerVar = newsPager;
            microTemplateId = 'homebloc_content_tpl';
            nbPage = $('section.blocNews ul.translateContentCommand').find('.translatecontent-nbPage').size();
            currentPage = $(pagerVar.params.pager).find('.selected').index(pagerVar.params.pager + ' ' + pagerVar.params.pageLink);
            ajaxUrl = '?ctrl=ajax_home&type=news&newsPerPage=' + displayVal + '&nbPage=' + nbPage;
            blocToReplace = '.blocNews .simpleListing';
            dataType = 'json';
            if (!userPref.blocNews) {
              userPref.blocNews = {};
            }
            userPref.blocNews.displayVal = displayVal;
            break;
          case 'blocForum':
            pagerVar = forumPager;
            currentPage = $(pagerVar.params.pager).find('.selected').index(pagerVar.params.pager + ' ' + pagerVar.params.pageLink);
            currentPage++;
            ajaxUrl = '?ctrl=ajax_home&type=forum4&topicsPerPage=' + displayVal + '&dateLocale=' + 'en_US' + '&page=' + currentPage;
            blocToReplace = '.blocForum .topicListing tbody';
            dataType = 'html';
            if (!userPref.blocForum) {
              userPref.blocForum = {};
            }
            userPref.blocForum.displayVal = displayVal;
            break;
          default:
            dataType = 'text';
            break;
        }
        // Create the cookie with the user preference
        document.cookie = userPrefCookieName + "=" + JSON.stringify(userPref);

        // Hide the content before the ajax request
        if(jQuery.support.opacity) {
          $(blocToReplace).animate({opacity:0}, 400, function() {});
        }
        else {
          $(blocToReplace).css({'visibility': 'hidden'});
        }

        // Get the content from the controller
        $.ajax({
          type: "GET",
          url: ajaxUrl,
          dataType: dataType,
          success: function(data) {
            if(data) {
              var params = { 'currentPage':currentPage, 'type':dataType, 'displayVal':displayVal, 'blocToReplace':blocToReplace, 'microTemplateId':microTemplateId, 'pagerVar':pagerVar };
              displayNResults(params, data);
            }

            // Display the content once the ajax request is done
            if(jQuery.support.opacity) {
              $(blocToReplace).animate({opacity:1}, 600);
            }
            else {
              $(blocToReplace).css({"visibility": "visible"});
            }
          }
        });
      }
    });

    // Treat the html content with the result
    function displayNResults(params, data) {
      switch(params.type) {
        case 'json':
          var microTemplateParams = {};
          microTemplateParams.content = data.slice(params.currentPage*params.displayVal, (params.currentPage*params.displayVal) + params.displayVal);
          $(params.blocToReplace)[0].innerHTML = BOM.Utils.templating.render(params.microTemplateId, microTemplateParams);
          params.pagerVar.params.jsonData = data;
          params.pagerVar.params.nbEltPerPage = params.displayVal;
          params.pagerVar.updateParams(params.pagerVar.params);
          break;
        case 'html':
          $(params.blocToReplace).html(data);
          params.pagerVar.params.nbEltPerPage = params.displayVal;
          params.pagerVar.params.url = '?ctrl=ajax_home&type=forum4&topicsPerPage=' + params.displayVal + '&dateLocale=' + 'en_US' + '&page=';
          params.pagerVar.updateParams(params.pagerVar.params);
          break;
        default:
          break;
      }
    }
  </script>

  //<![CDATA[
  

  function toggleVersions() {
    $('#lang_other').toggleClass('h');
    $('#arrow_toggle').toggleClass('arrow_left');
    return false;
  }

  // Xiti tracking
  var homepageVersion = 'Beta3';
  function trackClick(sectionId) {
    

    xt_med('C', '1', sectionId, 'N');
  }

  $('header').live('mousedown', function(evt) {
    var elt = evt.target;
    if( elt.tagName.toLowerCase()=='a' || $(elt).parents('a').length > 0) {
      trackClick(homepageVersion + '_Header_click');
    }
    else if( elt.tagName.toLowerCase()=='button' && $(elt).hasClass('searchBtn')) {
      trackClick(homepageVersion + '_Header_click');
    }
  });

  $('section.content').live('mousedown', function(evt) {
    var elt = evt.target;
    if( (elt.tagName.toLowerCase()=='a' && !$(elt).hasClass('noTracking') && !$(elt).hasClass('carousel-control'))|| $(elt).parents('a').length > 0 || (elt.tagName.toLowerCase()=='button' && $(elt).hasClass('submitLink'))) {
      var regExp = 'blocNewsLetter|blocForum|blocLatestArticles|blocTopics|blocVendorVoice|blocTomsGuideArticles|blocCharts|advertRight|blocWhitePapers|blocFollowUs|blocNews|blocTwitter';
      var sectionId = $(elt).parents('section').eq(0).attr('class').match(regExp);
      if(sectionId==null) {
        trackClick(homepageVersion + '_Other');
      }
      else {
        switch(sectionId[0]) {
          case 'blocNews':
            trackClick(homepageVersion + '_News');
            break;
          case 'blocForum':
            trackClick(homepageVersion  + '_Forum');
            break;
          case 'blocLatestArticles':
            trackClick(homepageVersion + '_Features');
            break;
          case 'blocTopics':
            trackClick(homepageVersion + '_Topics');
            break;
          case 'blocVendorVoice':
            trackClick(homepageVersion + '_Vendor_voice');
            break;
          case 'blocTomsGuideArticles':
            trackClick(homepageVersion + '_Misc_articles');
            break;
          case 'blocCharts':
            trackClick(homepageVersion + '_Misc_articles');
            break;
          case 'blocNewsLetter':
            trackClick(homepageVersion + '_Other');
            break;
          case 'blocFollowUs':
            trackClick(homepageVersion + '_Other');
            break;
          case 'blocTwitter':
            trackClick(homepageVersion + '_Other');
            break;
          case 'advertRight':
            break;
          case 'blocWhitePapers':
            break;
          default:
            trackClick(homepageVersion + '_Other');
            break;
        }
      }
    }
  });

  $('#bomFT').live('mousedown', function(evt) {
    var elt = evt.target;
    if( elt.tagName.toLowerCase()=='a' || $(elt).parents('a').length > 0) {
      trackClick(homepageVersion + '_Footer_click');
    }
  });
  // End of xiti tracking

  
  //]]>

 // Launch all the functions stored in BOM.gaStuff 
  BOM.gaStuff = BOM.gaStuff  || [];
  BOM.gaIsLoaded = function() {
    for (var i = 0; i < BOM.gaStuff.length; i++) {
      if (1 < BOM.gaStuff[i].length) {
        BOM.gaStuff[i][0](BOM.gaStuff[i][1]);
      } else {
        BOM.gaStuff[i][0]();
      }
    }
  };

  (function() {
    var ga = document.createElement('script'); 
    ga.type = 'text/javascript'; 
    ga.async = true;
    ga.src = ('https:' == document.location.protocol ? 'https://ssl' : 'http://www') + '.google-analytics.com/ga.js';
    
    var s = document.getElementsByTagName('script')[0]; 
    s.parentNode.insertBefore(ga, s);
    
    if (ga.addEventListener){

    } else if (ga.attachEvent){

      BOM.gaIsLoaded();
    }
  })();
